# Senior Internship Profiles

Generated from the 2021-2026 internship/job fair catalogs. Broad institutions such as UW, Fred Hutch, ISB, and Seattle Children's are split by mentor, lab, or contact group when the catalog data supports it.

Scanned 2022-2024 entries came from OCR and are marked in the website. Verify catalog page references before sending important emails.

Total profiles: 378
Total past placement examples: 551

## UW Elementary Particle Experiment Machine Learning Group - Shih-Chieh Hsu

Larger organization: UW Elementary Particle Experiment Group
Mentor/lab focus: Shih-Chieh Hsu
Best for: CS / AI / Data, Engineering / Physics, Research
Catalog categories: Research (w/ Computer Science & Engineering), Research, Computer Science and Engineering, Research: Physics/Computing Research, Physics, Research/Computer Science, Research/Computer Science & Engineering
Location: UW Seattle, University of Washington Physics Department, 1 weekly meeting in person at UW, rest remote, UW, remote, University of Washington-Seattle/Remote, University of Washington Physics and Astronomy Building, University of Washington, UW Physics and Astronomy Building (PAB) 3910 15th Ave NE, Seattle, WA 98195
Catalog years: 2026, 2025, 2024, 2023, 2022, 2021
Past placement examples: 18
Contacts:
- Shih-Chieh Hsu - schsu@uw.edu

What interns did:
The EPE-ML team applies machine learning techniques to known problems in particle physics, using data from the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) at CERN. After initial training, I was able to take ownership of two research projects, along with a team of a few other undergraduates. We had set times for biweekly status reports to Professor Hsu and our supervising postdoc, but other times for collaborative efforts between team members were highly flexible. The EPE ML Group, led by Professor Shih-Chieh Hsu in the University...

Notable activities:
- Experience in machine learning: TensorFlow; complex architectures like CNN; complex paradigms like GAN; many physics-motivated architectures like LBN, LGN, CWoLa, SALAD, DijetGAN - Crafting and executing a research project... I was involved with the classification of finger flexion decoding from electrocorticographic signals from the brain. - Familiarizing yourself with AI/ML concepts through case studies (stock market...

Outside source:
UW Physics profile for Shih-Chieh Hsu, whose listed work includes particle physics, ATLAS/LHC research, and machine-learning-related physics courses. (https://phys.washington.edu/people/shih-chieh-hsu)

## Smith Lab, Fred Hutchinson Cancer Center - Gerry Smith

Larger organization: Fred Hutchinson Cancer Center
Mentor/lab focus: Gerry Smith
Best for: Biomedical / Health, Research, CS / AI / Data
Catalog categories: Research, Bio/Medical, Medical/Health Sciences
Location: Seattle, Downtown Seattle, SeattleJ WA, Seattle, WA, Weintraub Building, Seattle, Seattle, SLU
Catalog years: 2025, 2024, 2023, 2022, 2021
Past placement examples: 6
Contacts:
- Professor Gerry Smith - gsmith@fredhutch.org

What interns did:
The Smith Lab at Fred Hutch has current focus on recombination genetics in Escherichia coli and Schizosaccharomyces pombe. As a researcher, I've focused my efforts on the RecBCD enzyme in E. coli, producing data and compiling a manuscript to disprove commonly held, yet incorrect, assumptions about the critical recombination enzyme. As a diligent worker, my mentor was extremely understanding regarding my schedule provided I communicate my responsibilities ahead of time. The Fred Hutch Cancer Center is a biomedical...

Notable activities:
- Developing prospective research questions and planning out lab work - Using industry standard programs and services such as ClusPro, SnapGene, PyMol, NCBI, GeneBank, etc. - Computational genetic comparisons and analysis with python and Java - Learning and applying different techniques used by S. pombe geneticists - Reading and discussing papers with my mentor - Enjoying donuts with lab scientists! Practical microbiological...

Outside source:
Official Fred Hutch pages describe a Seattle cancer research and care center with a long research history, global reach, thousands of employees, and Nobel Prize-winning scientific work. (https://www.fredhutch.org/en/about.html)

Since C elegans have short lifespans (2-3 days) and are relatively simple organisms (with only approximately 1000 cells), they are useful for testing the effects of anti-aging drugs or knocking out specific genes to study their... Through this internship, I have learned many practical research skills and I have developed a better understanding of how scientific...

Notable activities:
- I score Wormbot images of C elegans and creating graphs to communicate the data. - I help create a general database of the efficacy of various natural products in treating different symptoms. For instance, if I find a journal article that describes a controlled trial testing the effects of ashwagandha on reducing anxiety, I summarize the information and add it to the spreadsheet. - Based on the research articles we read, we...

Outside source:
Large public research university. Broad UW placements are split by the catalog mentor, lab, department, or source-backed contact group. (https://www.washington.edu/)

The Lampe laboratory performs studies to find blood tests or protein biomarkers that can indicate if and where a person has cancer and if it is present, how to best treat it. Specifically, they are working to find early detection, recurrence or response biomarkers of colon, breast, and lung cancer. Once the biomarker is defined, they make drugs based on that biomarker so the tumors can be directly attacked.

## Fred Hutchinson Cancer Center - Mark Roth

Larger organization: Fred Hutchinson Cancer Center
Mentor/lab focus: Mark Roth
Best for: Biomedical / Health, Research
Catalog categories: Research: Bio/Medical
Location: On Site: 1100 Fairview Ave N, Seattle, WA 98109, Roth Lab
Catalog years: 2026
Past placement examples: 1
Contacts:
- Mark Roth - mroth@fredhutch.org

What interns did:
I study the phenomenon of suspended animation in the nematode C. When deprived of oxygen, adult nematodes can survive in an alternative death-like state for anywhere from 48 to 72 hours at room temperature. This phenomenon, termed suspended animation, can be replicated in other animals - including humans – and can prove useful in industry.

Notable activities:
The Roth lab is unique in how it conducts science. Rather than searching for genotype- phenotype correlations, my mentor finds it more convenient to assay for life and death directly.

Outside source:
Official Fred Hutch pages describe a Seattle cancer research and care center with a long research history, global reach, thousands of employees, and Nobel Prize-winning scientific work. (https://www.fredhutch.org/en/about.html)

People who went here before:
- Evan Wang (2026) - Research: Bio/Medical [Internship Catalogue 2026, p. 46]
